\doxysubsection{详细描述}
\subsubsection*{template$<$typename \+\_\+\+Scalar, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae4f82344f573c70aa1066a2394bba345}{int}} \+\_\+\+Options, typename \+\_\+\+Storage\+Index$>$\newline
class Eigen\+::\+Sparse\+Matrix$<$ \+\_\+\+Scalar, \+\_\+\+Options, \+\_\+\+Storage\+Index $>$}
\doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} versatible sparse matrix representation 

This class implements a more versatile variants of the common {\itshape compressed} row/column storage format. Each colmun\textquotesingle{}s (resp. row) non zeros are stored as a pair of value with associated row (resp. colmiun) index. All the non zeros are stored in a single large buffer. Unlike the {\itshape compressed} format, there might be extra space inbetween the nonzeros of two successive colmuns (resp. rows) such that insertion of new non-\/zero can be done with limited memory reallocation and copies.

\doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} call to the function \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_a5ff54ffc10296f9466dc81fa888733fd}{make\+Compressed()} turns the matrix into the standard {\itshape compressed} format compatible with many library.

More details on this storage sceheme are given in the \doxylink{group___tutorial_sparse}{manual pages}.


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em \+\_\+\+Scalar} & the scalar type, i.\+e. the type of the coefficients \\
\hline
{\em \+\_\+\+Options} & Union of bit flags controlling the storage scheme. Currently the only possibility is Col\+Major or Row\+Major. The default is 0 which means column-\/major. \\
\hline
{\em \+\_\+\+Storage\+Index} & the type of the indices. It has to be a {\bfseries{signed}} type (e.\+g., short, int, std\+::ptrdiff\+\_\+t). Default is {\ttfamily int}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
In Eigen 3.\+2, the undocumented type {\ttfamily \doxylink{struct_eigen_1_1_eigen_base_a554f30542cc2316add4b1ea0a492ff02}{Sparse\+Matrix\+::\+Index}} was improperly defined as the storage index type (e.\+g., int), whereas it is now (starting from Eigen 3.\+3) deprecated and always defined as \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Eigen\+::\+Index}. Codes making use of {\ttfamily \doxylink{struct_eigen_1_1_eigen_base_a554f30542cc2316add4b1ea0a492ff02}{Sparse\+Matrix\+::\+Index}}, might thus likely have to be changed to use {\ttfamily \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base_a0b540ba724726ebe953f8c0df06081ed}{Sparse\+Matrix\+::\+Storage\+Index}} instead.
\end{DoxyWarning}
This class can be extended with the help of the plugin mechanism described on the page \doxylink{TopicCustomizing_Plugins}{Extending Matrix\+Base (and other classes)} by defining the preprocessor symbol {\ttfamily EIGEN\+\_\+\+SPARSEMATRIX\+\_\+\+PLUGIN}.

\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_product}{Scalar}} \& \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix}{Eigen\+::\+Sparse\+Matrix}}$<$ \+\_\+\+Scalar, \+\_\+\+Options, \+\_\+\+Storage\+Index $>$\+::coeff\+Ref (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{row}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{col}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
a non-\/const reference to the value of the matrix at position {\itshape i}, {\itshape j} 
\end{DoxyReturn}
If the element does not exist then it is inserted via the \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_aae45e3b5fec7f6a0cdd10eec7c6d3666}{insert(\+Index,\+Index)} function which itself turns the matrix into a non compressed form if that was not the case.

This is a O(log(nnz\+\_\+j)) operation (binary search) plus the cost of \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_aae45e3b5fec7f6a0cdd10eec7c6d3666}{insert(\+Index,\+Index)} function if the element does not already exist. \Hypertarget{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_a87ff49d0917b31f98862b661a5d72eec}\index{Eigen::SparseMatrix$<$ \_Scalar, \_Options, \_StorageIndex $>$@{Eigen::SparseMatrix$<$ \_Scalar, \_Options, \_StorageIndex $>$}!collapseDuplicates@{collapseDuplicates}}
\index{collapseDuplicates@{collapseDuplicates}!Eigen::SparseMatrix$<$ \_Scalar, \_Options, \_StorageIndex $>$@{Eigen::SparseMatrix$<$ \_Scalar, \_Options, \_StorageIndex $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{collapseDuplicates()}{collapseDuplicates()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_a87ff49d0917b31f98862b661a5d72eec}

\Hypertarget{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_a9dc538b2c1fe9027ba58f31ee83b2ff1}\index{Eigen::SparseMatrix$<$ \_Scalar, \_Options, \_StorageIndex $>$@{Eigen::SparseMatrix$<$ \_Scalar, \_Options, \_StorageIndex $>$}!conservativeResize@{conservativeResize}}
\index{conservativeResize@{conservativeResize}!Eigen::SparseMatrix$<$ \_Scalar, \_Options, \_StorageIndex $>$@{Eigen::SparseMatrix$<$ \_Scalar, \_Options, \_StorageIndex $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{conservativeResize()}{conservativeResize()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_a9dc538b2c1fe9027ba58f31ee83b2ff1} 
template$<$typename \+\_\+\+Scalar, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae4f82344f573c70aa1066a2394bba345}{int}} \+\_\+\+Options, typename \+\_\+\+Storage\+Index$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix}{Eigen\+::\+Sparse\+Matrix}}$<$ \+\_\+\+Scalar, \+\_\+\+Options, \+\_\+\+Storage\+Index $>$\+::conservative\+Resize (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{rows}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{cols}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Resizes the matrix to a {\itshape rows} x {\itshape cols} matrix leaving old values untouched.

If the sizes of the matrix are decreased, then the matrix is turned to {\bfseries{uncompressed-\/mode}} and the storage of the out of bounds coefficients is kept and reserved. Call \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_a5ff54ffc10296f9466dc81fa888733fd}{make\+Compressed()} to pack the entries and squeeze extra memory.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{参见}
\doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_a1518e58ac49bed0e2385b722a034f7d3}{reserve()}, \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_ad3c7416090f913e8685523cb3ab7c2f7}{set\+Zero()}, \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_a5ff54ffc10296f9466dc81fa888733fd}{make\+Compressed()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_aae45e3b5fec7f6a0cdd10eec7c6d3666} 
template$<$typename \+\_\+\+Scalar, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae4f82344f573c70aa1066a2394bba345}{int}} \+\_\+\+Options, typename \+\_\+\+Storage\+Index$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix}{Sparse\+Matrix}}$<$ \+\_\+\+Scalar, \+\_\+\+Options, \+\_\+\+Storage\+Index $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_a052eb942d12b6404aade6fae4b075fb9}{\+::\+Scalar}} \& \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix}{Eigen\+::\+Sparse\+Matrix}}$<$ \+\_\+\+Scalar, \+\_\+\+Options, \+\_\+\+Storage\+Index $>$\+::insert (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{row}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{col}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
a reference to a novel non zero coefficient with coordinates {\itshape row} x {\itshape col}. The non zero coefficient must {\bfseries{not}} already exist.
\end{DoxyReturn}
If the matrix {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this} is in compressed mode, then {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this} is turned into uncompressed mode while reserving room for 2 x this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}\doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_a0f42824d4a06ee1d1f6afbc4551c5896}{inner\+Size()} non zeros if \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_a1518e58ac49bed0e2385b722a034f7d3}{reserve(\+Index)} has not been called earlier. In this case, the insertion procedure is optimized for a {\itshape sequential} insertion mode where elements are assumed to be inserted by increasing outer-\/indices.

If that\textquotesingle{}s not the case, then it is strongly recommended to either use a triplet-\/list to assemble the matrix, or to first call reserve(const Sizes\+Type \&) to reserve the appropriate number of non-\/zero elements per inner vector.

Assuming memory has been appropriately reserved, this function performs a sorted insertion in O(1) if the elements of each inner vector are inserted in increasing inner index order, and in O(nnz\+\_\+j) for a random insertion. 函数调用图\+:

\Hypertarget{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_acc35051d698e3973f1de5b9b78dbe345}\index{Eigen::SparseMatrix$<$ \_Scalar, \_Options, \_StorageIndex $>$@{Eigen::SparseMatrix$<$ \_Scalar, \_Options, \_StorageIndex $>$}!setFromTriplets@{setFromTriplets}}
\index{setFromTriplets@{setFromTriplets}!Eigen::SparseMatrix$<$ \_Scalar, \_Options, \_StorageIndex $>$@{Eigen::SparseMatrix$<$ \_Scalar, \_Options, \_StorageIndex $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setFromTriplets()}{setFromTriplets()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_acc35051d698e3973f1de5b9b78dbe345} 
template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_product}{Scalar}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae4f82344f573c70aa1066a2394bba345}{int}} \+\_\+\+Options, typename \+\_\+\+Storage\+Index$>$ \\
template$<$typename Input\+Iterators$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix}{Eigen\+::\+Sparse\+Matrix}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_product}{Scalar}}, \+\_\+\+Options, \+\_\+\+Storage\+Index $>$\+::set\+From\+Triplets (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const Input\+Iterators \&}]{begin}{, }\item[{const Input\+Iterators \&}]{end}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Fill the matrix {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this} with the list of {\itshape triplets} defined by the iterator range {\itshape begin} -\/ {\itshape end}.

\doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} {\itshape triplet} is a tuple (i,j,value) defining a non-\/zero element. The input list of triplets does not have to be sorted, and can contains duplicated elements. In any case, the result is a {\bfseries{sorted}} and {\bfseries{compressed}} sparse matrix where the duplicates have been summed up. This is a {\itshape O(n)} operation, with {\itshape n} the number of triplet elements. The initial contents of {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this} is destroyed. The matrix {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this} must be properly resized beforehand using the \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_a6abf1015a0243be97648e106a17b01ea}{Sparse\+Matrix(\+Index,\+Index)} constructor, or the \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_af88551f30202341b7cc24cfadabdec5c}{resize(\+Index,\+Index)} method. The sizes are not extracted from the triplet list.

The {\itshape Input\+Iterators} \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base_ac254d3b61718ebc2136d27bac043dcb7}{value\+\_\+type} must provide the following interface\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base_a477b2830b50a0a04260463d6f8def336}{Scalar}}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_abe8e049f756b5ba547bda825af81b645}{value}}()\ \textcolor{keyword}{const};\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ the\ value}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base_a477b2830b50a0a04260463d6f8def336}{Scalar}}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base_ac0a5563ed3f243f013fb9d2c17e230d0}{row}}()\ \textcolor{keyword}{const};\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ the\ row\ index\ i}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base_a477b2830b50a0a04260463d6f8def336}{Scalar}}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_base_a8f4eaa3c3921ef3823ffc69ebcc356af}{col}}()\ \textcolor{keyword}{const};\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ the\ column\ index\ j}}

\end{DoxyCode}
 See for instance the \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_triplet}{Eigen\+::\+Triplet} template class.

Here is a typical usage example\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{typedef}\ Triplet<double>\ \mbox{\hyperlink{test__overwrite__node_8cpp_a0acb682b8260ab1c60b918599864e2e5}{T}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{std::vector<T>\ tripletList;}
\DoxyCodeLine{triplets.reserve(estimation\_of\_entries);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(...)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ tripletList.push\_back(\mbox{\hyperlink{test__overwrite__node_8cpp_a0acb682b8260ab1c60b918599864e2e5}{T}}(\mbox{\hyperlink{_bi_c_g_s_t_a_b__step__by__step_8cpp_acb559820d9ca11295b4500f179ef6392}{i}},\mbox{\hyperlink{tut__arithmetic__redux__minmax_8cpp_a39513f0f8d942bf9ef17b2e87ac6d34e}{j}},v\_ij));}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{SparseMatrixType\ \mbox{\hyperlink{_angle_axis__mimic__euler_8cpp_ab3cd915d758008bd19d0f2428fbb354a}{m}}(\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_a62e61bb861eee306d5b069ce652b5aa5}{rows}},\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_sparse_matrix_aa391750e3c530227e4a5c3c52e959975}{cols}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{_angle_axis__mimic__euler_8cpp_ab3cd915d758008bd19d0f2428fbb354a}{m}}.setFromTriplets(tripletList.begin(),\ tripletList.end());}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ m\ is\ ready\ to\ go!}}

\end{DoxyCode}


\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
The list of triplets is read multiple times (at least twice). Therefore, it is not recommended to define an abstract iterator over a complex data-\/structure that would be expensive to evaluate. The triplets should rather be explicitely stored into a std\+::vector for instance. 
\end{DoxyWarning}
